<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" width="44" height="44"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has articles on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bat_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:bat (disambiguation)">bat</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bat_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:bat (disambiguation)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg/250px-Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg/375px-Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/58/Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg 2x" data-file-width="492" data-file-height="792" width="250" height="402"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mariana_Fruit_Bat.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A <b>bat</b></div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">băt</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bæt/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Dialectal variant (akin to dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=natt-batta&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="natt-batta (page does not exist)">natt-batta</a></i>) of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/bakke#Middle_English" title="bakke">bakke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/balke#Middle_English" title="balke">balke</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-osw"><a href="/w/index.php?title=natbakka&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="natbakka (page does not exist)">natbakka</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Danish language">Old Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-oda"><a href="/w/index.php?title=nathbakk%C3%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="nathbakkæ (page does not exist)">nathbakkæ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">night-flapper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/w/index.php?title=le%C3%B0rblaka&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="leðrblaka (page does not exist)">leðrblaka</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leather-flapper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">bat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bats#English" title="bats">bats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of the flying <a href="/wiki/mammal" title="mammal">mammals</a> of the order <a href="/wiki/Chiroptera" title="Chiroptera">Chiroptera</a>, usually small and <a href="/wiki/nocturnal" title="nocturnal">nocturnal</a>, <a href="/wiki/insectivorous" title="insectivorous">insectivorous</a> or <a href="/wiki/frugivorous" title="frugivorous">frugivorous</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1920</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Roberts_Rinehart" class="extiw" title="w:Mary Roberts Rinehart">Mary Roberts Rinehart</a>; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avery_Hopwood" class="extiw" title="w:Avery Hopwood">Avery Hopwood</a>,  chapter I, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Bat_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:The Bat (play)">The Bat: A Novel from the Play</a></cite> (Dell Book; 241), New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dell_Publishing" class="extiw" title="w:Dell Publishing">Dell Publishing Company</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/20230794">20230794</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://babel.hathitrust.org/cgi/pt?id=hvd.hwptej;view=1up;seq=5">page 01</a>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The Bat—they called him the Bat. Like a <b>bat</b> he chose the night hours for his work of rapine; like a <b>bat</b> he struck and vanished, pouncingly, noiselessly; like a <b>bat</b> he never showed himself to the face of the day.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b>, Suemedha Sood, <span style="font-family:monospace;">(bbc.co.uk)</span> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/travel/blog/20120209-travelwise-texas-love-bats">Travelwise: Texas love bats</a> [sic]
<dl><dd>As well as being worth millions of dollars to the Texan agriculture industry, these mammals are worth millions of dollars to the state’s tourism industry. Texas is home to the world’s largest known <b>bat</b> colony (in Comal County), and the world’s largest urban <b>bat</b> colony (in Austin). <b>Bat</b> watching is a common activity, with the Texas Parks and Wildlife Department offering more <b>bat</b>-viewing sites than anywhere else in the US.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An old woman.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bill_Oddie" class="extiw" title="w:Bill Oddie">Bill Oddie</a>,  <cite>Gripping Yarns</cite>, page 196:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"Isn't it lovely?" I smiled and thought: "Yes it is. It's also a Blackbird, you silly old <b>bat</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/bat#Middle_English" title="bat">bat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/batte#Middle_English" title="batte">batte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/batt#Old_English" title="batt">batt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bat, club, cudgel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span> origin, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Breton language">Old Breton</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="obt"><a href="/wiki/bath#Old_Breton" title="bath">bath</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">club, cudgel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Breton language">Breton</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="br"><a href="/w/index.php?title=bazh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="bazh (page does not exist)">bazh</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swagger stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">bat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bats#English" title="bats">bats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/club" title="club">club</a> made of wood or aluminium used for striking the ball in sports such as <a href="/wiki/baseball" title="baseball">baseball</a>, <a href="/wiki/softball" title="softball">softball</a> and <a href="/wiki/cricket" title="cricket">cricket</a>.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/turn" title="turn">turn</a> at <a href="/wiki/hitting" title="hitting">hitting</a> the <a href="/wiki/ball" title="ball">ball</a> with a bat in a <a href="/wiki/game" title="game">game</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You've been in for ages. Can I have a <b>bat</b> now?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/two-up" title="two-up">two-up</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The piece of wood on which the <a href="/wiki/spinner" title="spinner">spinner</a> places the coins and then uses for throwing them.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mining#Noun" title="mining">mining</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/shale" title="shale">Shale</a> or <a href="/wiki/bituminous" title="bituminous">bituminous</a> shale.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_quotation/Kirwan" title="Category:Requests for quotation/Kirwan">find and add</a> a quotation of Kirwan to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/sheet" title="sheet">sheet</a> of <a href="/wiki/cotton" title="cotton">cotton</a> used for filling <a href="/wiki/quilt" title="quilt">quilts</a> or <a href="/wiki/comfortable" title="comfortable">comfortables</a>; <a href="/wiki/batting" title="batting">batting</a>.</li>
<li>A part of a <a href="/wiki/brick" title="brick">brick</a> with one whole end.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/stroke" title="stroke">stroke</a>; a <a href="/wiki/sharp" title="sharp">sharp</a> <a href="/wiki/blow" title="blow">blow</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialect</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stroke of work.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Rate of motion; speed.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1842</b>, <i>Sporting Magazine</i> (page 251)
<dl><dd>On starting, The Nun led at a very slow pace for a quarter of a mile, when the Shrigley colt made running at a good <b>bat</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1898</b>, unknown author, <i>Pall Mall Magazine</i>
<dl><dd>a vast host of fowl <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> making at full <b>bat</b> for the North Sea.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/spree" title="spree">spree</a>; a <a href="/wiki/jollification" title="jollification">jollification</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialect</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Manner; rate; condition; state of health.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Synonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">two-up</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/kip#English" title="kip">kip</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/stick#English" title="stick">stick</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/kylie#English" title="kylie">kylie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/lannet#English" title="lannet">lannet</a></span></li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">bat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bats#English" title="bats">bats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/batting#English" title="batting">batting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/batted#English" title="batted">batted</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hit with a bat or (figuratively) as if with a bat.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He <b>batted</b> the ball away with a satisfying thwack.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We <b>batted</b> a few ideas around.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English-take_a_turn_at_hitting"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take a turn at hitting a ball with a bat in sports like <a href="/wiki/cricket" title="cricket">cricket</a>, <a href="/wiki/baseball" title="baseball">baseball</a> and <a href="/wiki/softball" title="softball">softball</a>, as opposed to <a href="/wiki/field" title="field">fielding</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/strike" title="strike">strike</a> or <a href="/wiki/swipe" title="swipe">swipe</a> as though with a bat.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The cat <b>batted</b> at the toy.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Possibly a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bate#English" title="bate">bate</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">bat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bats#English" title="bats">bats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/batting#English" title="batting">batting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/batted#English" title="batted">batted</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/flutter" title="flutter">flutter</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>bat</b> one's eyelashes</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialect</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/wink" title="wink">wink</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialect</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/bate" title="bate">bate</a> or flutter, as a <a href="/wiki/hawk" title="hawk">hawk</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually with 'around' or 'about'</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To flit quickly from place to place.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I've spent all week <b>batting</b> around the country.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Most commonly used in the phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat_an_eye#English" title="bat an eye">bat an eye</a></i>, and variants thereof.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_4">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Derived terms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat_an_eye#English" title="bat an eye">bat an eye</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat_an_eyelash#English" title="bat an eyelash">bat an eyelash</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat_an_eyelid#English" title="bat an eyelid">bat an eyelid</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Etymology 4">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/b%C3%A2t#French" title="bât">bât</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/bast#Old_French" title="bast">bast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Latin/bastum&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Latin/bastum (page does not exist)">*bastum</a></i>, form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Latin/bastare" title="Reconstruction:Latin/bastare">*bastāre</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CE%B2%CE%B1%CF%83%CF%84%CE%AC%CE%B6%CF%89#Ancient_Greek" title="βαστάζω">βαστάζω</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="grc-Latn">bastázō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lift, carry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/baton#English" title="baton">baton</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/baston#English" title="baston">baston</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/batto#Latin" title="batto">battō</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/battuo#Latin" title="battuo">battuō</a></i>. Compare Daco-<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro"><a href="/wiki/bate#Romanian" title="bate">bate</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro"><a href="/wiki/bat#Romanian" title="bat">bat</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="rup">bat</strong> (<i>third-person singular present indicative</i> <b><a href="/wiki/bati" title="bati">bati</a>/<a href="/wiki/bate" title="bate">bate</a></b>, <i>past participle</i> <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=b%C3%A3tut%C3%A3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="bãtutã (page does not exist)">bãtutã</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>I <a href="/wiki/beat" title="beat">beat</a>, <a href="/wiki/hit" title="hit">hit</a>, <a href="/wiki/strike" title="strike">strike</a>.</li>
<li>I <a href="/wiki/defeat" title="defeat">defeat</a>.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Basque">Basque</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Basque">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From a reduced form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Basque_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Basque language">Proto-Basque</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="euq-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Basque/bade&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Basque/bade (page does not exist)">*bade</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, present also in <i class="Latn mention" lang="eu"><a href="/wiki/bederatzi#Basque" title="bederatzi">bederatzi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="eu"><a href="/w/index.php?title=bedera&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="bedera (page does not exist)">bedera</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">same; everyone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[3]</a></sup> Compared by Eduardo Orduña and Joan Ferrer to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iberian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Iberian language">Iberian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="xib"><a href="/wiki/ban#Iberian" title="ban">ban</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[5]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Basque" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Basque">standard</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basque_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Basque phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bat/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat#English" title="bat">bat</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="da">bat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>singular definite</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da def|s-form-of" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/battet#Danish" title="battet">battet</a></b>, <i>plural indefinite</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da indef|p-form-of" lang="da"><strong class="selflink">bat</strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da indef|p-form-of" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/bats#Danish" title="bats">bats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat#English" title="bat">bat</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a club for striking a ball</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg/220px-Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg/330px-Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg/440px-Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1500" width="220" height="220"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Orthopygia.glaucinalis.7371.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>bat</div></div></div>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="jam"><strong class="selflink">bat</strong></strong>&nbsp;(<i>plural</i>: bat dem, <i>quantified</i>: bat)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/moth" title="moth">moth</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">nocturnal insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2003</b>,  Amber Wilson,  <cite>Jamaica: The Land</cite> (in English), page 30:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“Hundreds of species of butterflies and moths live in Jamaica. Jamaicans call large moths "<b>bats</b>." The black witch moth is known as "the duppy bat." A duppy is a spirit in Jamaican culture that sometimes causes mischief. Duppy bats have brown [...]”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="jam">Duppy <b>bat</b> still a fly like hawk.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Black witch <b>moths</b> are still flying around like hawks.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:A_modern_Cricket_bat_(back_view).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg/220px-A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg" decoding="async" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg/330px-A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg/440px-A_modern_Cricket_bat_%28back_view%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1536" data-file-height="2048" width="220" height="293"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:A_modern_Cricket_bat_(back_view).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>bat</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat#English" title="bat">bat</a></i>.

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="jam"><strong class="selflink">bat</strong></strong>&nbsp;(<i>plural</i>: bat dem, <i>quantified</i>: bat)
</p>
<ol><li><a class="mw-selflink selflink">bat</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">instrument for hitting or striking</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="jam">When yu get one lick from me wid di <b>bat</b>... yu wi know.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If I hit you once with this <b>bat</b>, you'll understand.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_English">Middle English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: Middle English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_5">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=97" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/batt#Old_English" title="batt">batt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span>; influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/batte#Old_French" title="batte">batte</a></i>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=99" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Middle_English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Middle English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bat/</span>, <span class="IPA">/bɔt/</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=100" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="enm">bat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/battes#Middle_English" title="battes">battes</a></span></b> or <b><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/botten#Middle_English" title="botten">botten</a></span></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/mace" title="mace">mace</a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bat#English" title="bat">bat</a></span>, or <a href="/wiki/morningstar" title="morningstar">morningstar</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">blunt weapon</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pole or stick used for other</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English#Late_Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Late Middle English</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A strike or hit from a weapon.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English#Late_Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Late Middle English</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A clump of soft material.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_English">Old English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=106" title="Edit section: Old English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=107" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/bait" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/bait">*bait</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_10">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=108" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Old_English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Old English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bɑːt/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_15">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=109" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang">bāt</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latinx" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/batas#Old_English" title="batas">bātas</a></b>)
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_6">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=123" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_17">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=124" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_7">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=140" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%D8%A8%D8%A7%D8%B5%D8%AF%DB%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="باصدی (page does not exist)">باصدی</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="ota-Latn"><a href="/w/index.php?title=bast%C4%B1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="bastı (page does not exist)">bastı</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota"><a href="/wiki/%D8%A8%D8%A7%D8%B5%D9%85%D9%82#Ottoman_Turkish" title="باصمق">باصمق</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="ota-Latn"><a href="/wiki/basmak#Turkish" title="basmak">basmak</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_14">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=141" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Serbo-Croatian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Serbo-Croatian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bâːt/</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_21">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=142" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sh">bȃt</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>Cyrillic spelling</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/%D0%B1%D0%B0%D1%82#Serbo-Croatian" title="бат">ба̑т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The tramp of heavy footsteps, as in a military march
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1939</b>, Čedomir Minderović, <i>Crven je istok i zapad</i>:
<dl><dd>Napred, sve bliže i bliže, / Čuje se koraka <b>bat</b>. / Glas milijona se diže: / Dole fašizam i rat!
<dl><dd>Forward, ever closer and closer, / the <b>tramp</b> of footsteps is heard. / The voice of millions is raised: / Down with fascism and war!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The tramp of horses’ hooves</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_24">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=159" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Zhuang">Zhuang</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=166" title="Edit section: Zhuang">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_17">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=167" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Zhuang" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Zhuang">Standard Zhuang</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zhuang_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Zhuang phonology">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/paːt˧˥/</span></li>

<li>Hyphenation: bat</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_8">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=168" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh"><a href="/wiki/%E7%BC%BD#Chinese" title="缽">缽</a></span> (<i><span class="tr Latn"><span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Middle Chinese">MC</span> puɑt̚</span></i>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_28">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=169" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="za">bat</strong> (<i>Sawndip forms</i> <b class="Hani" lang="za"><a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%B3#Zhuang" title="朳">朳</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Hani" lang="za"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%F0%A5%90%99&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="𥐙 (page does not exist)">𥐙</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Hani" lang="za"><a href="/wiki/%E9%88%B8#Zhuang" title="鈸">鈸</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Hani" lang="za"><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AD#Zhuang" title="叭">叭</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Hani" lang="za"><a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%94#Zhuang" title="拔">拔</a></b>, <i>old orthography</i> <b class="Latn" lang="za"><strong class="selflink">bat</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/basin" title="basin">basin</a>; <a href="/wiki/bowl" title="bowl">bowl</a>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_8">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=bat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=172" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
